id="radix-_R_fqinpfiulb_" hidden="" data-toc-popover="" class="overflow-hidden flex flex-col px-4 max-h-[50vh] md:px-6"></div></header><article class="flex min-w-0 w-full flex-col gap-4 pt-8 px-4 md:px-6 md:mx-auto"><span class="hidden lg:block text-sublabel text-accent !m-0 !my-0 !p-0">Guides</span><div class="prose flex-1"><h1 class="text-[1.75em] font-semibold">Advanced: Build Stedi guides</h1><p>You can create, import, and customize guides for any of the 300+ X12 transaction sets.</p>
<p>Most users don&#x27;t need to build custom guides - we strongly recommend importing your trading partner&#x27;s guides from the <a href="https://www.stedi.com/edi/network" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Stedi Network</a> into your account for free. If you&#x27;re sending or receiving X12 HIPAA transactions, you definitely don&#x27;t need to build custom guides - you should use the pre-built <a href="https://www.stedi.com/edi/network/hipaa" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">X12 HIPAA guides</a> in the network as is.</p>
<p>However, many logistics and retail trading partners send EDI files that are not 100% compliant with their official guide for a transaction set. For example, they may use different codes for an element. In these cases, you can edit existing guides so that they accurately represent the EDI files you receive.</p>
<span class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg flex gap-3 border border-emerald-100 bg-emerald-50 dark:border-emerald-950 dark:bg-emerald-500/10" data-callout-type="tip"><span class="flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-6 flex items-center justify-center text-emerald-700 dark:text-emerald-300" data-component-part="callout-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon "><path d="M11 18H7.94101C7.64391 16.7274 6.30412 15.6857 5.75395 14.9992C4.65645 13.6297 4 11.8915 4 10C4 5.58172 7.58172 2 12 2C16.4183 2 20 5.58172 20 10C20 11.8925 19.3428 13.6315 18.2443 15.0014C17.6944 15.687 16.3558 16.7276 16.059 18H13V13H11V18ZM16 20V21C16 22.1046 15.1046 23 14 23H10C8.89543 23 8 22.1046 8 21V20H16Z"></path></svg></span><span class="prose min-w-0 w-full text-emerald-900 dark:text-emerald-200" data-component-part="callout-content"><p><strong>Not sure what to fix?</strong> If you received a guide-related file execution
error, <a href="https://www.stedi.com/contact" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">contact us</a> for help updating your
guide to fix the issue.</p></span></span>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="edit-existing-guides"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#edit-existing-guides"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Edit existing guides</a></h2>
<p>Go to your <a href="https://portal.stedi.com/app/guides" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Stedi account</a> and find the guide you want to edit.</p>
<p>To edit, click the <strong>ellipses (…)</strong> next to the guide and select <strong>Edit</strong>. The guide opens in the guide builder.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="create-guides"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#create-guides"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Create guides</a></h2>
<p>You can create a custom guide from the base specification for a transaction set from any X12 release. To create a guide:</p>
<ol>
<li>Go to your <a href="https://portal.stedi.com/app" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Stedi account</a> and click <strong>Create guide</strong>.</li>
<li>Select an <strong>X12 Release</strong> and the <strong>Transaction Set</strong> base specfication you want to customize.</li>
<li>Enter a unique <strong>Name</strong> for your guide and click <strong>Create</strong>. The new guide opens in the guide builder.</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="lock-guides"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#lock-guides"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Lock guides</a></h2>
<p>When you&#x27;re finished editing, you can lock a guide to prevent further updates. Locking helps prevent accidental changes or deletions to guides in production.</p>
<p>Any user in your Stedi account can lock guides, but only an account admin can unlock guides.</p>
<p>To lock a guide, go to the <strong>Actions</strong> menu and select <strong>Lock</strong>. No one can update, delete, or publish a locked guide. However, you can duplicate locked guides, if needed.</p>
<p>To unlock the guide, an admin can go to the <strong>Actions</strong> menu and select <strong>Unlock</strong>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="segments-and-loops"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#segments-and-loops"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Segments and Loops</a></h2>
<p>By default, the guide builder only lists the <a href="https://www.stedi.com/docs/edi-platform/edi-essentials/x12/segments/what-is-a-segment" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">segments</a> required in the base transaction set. You can add additional segments to your custom guide.</p>
<p>To add additional segments:</p>
<ol>
<li>Click either <strong>Heading</strong>, <strong>Detail</strong>, or <strong>Summary</strong> in the left sidebar to view a list of the possible segments for that section.</li>
<li>Click the box next to each segment to change whether it is included in the transaction set.<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><code>R</code>: Required. Note: Some PDF implementation guides use a designation of <code>M</code> (for Mandatory) instead. In these cases, <code>R</code> is still the appropriate choice.</li>
<li><code>O</code>: Optional.</li>
<li><code>N</code>: Not used by this implementation guide.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="hierarchical-levels"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#hierarchical-levels"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Hierarchical Levels</a></h3>
<p>An <code>HL</code> segment identifies dependencies between hierarchically related data segments. For example, there may be hierarchical relationships between components of packing information in an <a href="https://www.stedi.com/edi/x12/transaction-set/856" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">856 Ship Notice</a>.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="example-use-case"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#example-use-case"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Example use case</a></h4>
<p>Consider the following hierarchical information about customer grocery orders.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>ORD02208</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ├── Package</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      ├── Milk</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The following EDI example shows the HL loops that define this information.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>HL*1**O*1~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>PRF*ORD02208***20220815~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>HL*2*1*P*1~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>TD1*CTN*1~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>REF*CN*1B487311569~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>HL*3*2*I*0~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>LIN*D002*BN*75206331361~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>SN1**1*EA~</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>PID*F*TRN***MILK~</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The first <code>HL</code> segment defines the order at the highest level of the hierarchy. It has four elements.</p>
<div class="relative overflow-auto prose-no-margin my-6"><table><thead><tr><th>Element</th><th>Name</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>HL-01</code></td><td>ID Number</td><td>Identifies this entry of the HL loop.</td></tr><tr><td><code>HL-02</code></td><td>Parent ID Number</td><td>The ID Number of the order that this package relates to.</td></tr><tr><td><code>HL-03</code></td><td>Level Code</td><td>Specifies the type of the entry. In this case, a package.</td></tr><tr><td><code>HL-04</code></td><td>Child Code</td><td>Specifies whether this entry has children. <code>1</code> means yes.</td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<p>Then, the document continues:</p>
<ul>
<li>The <code>PRF</code> segment contains information about the order itself, including the order number <code>ORD02208</code>.</li>
<li>The <code>HL</code> segment repeats when the order becomes a package, and the package itself is described by the segments <code>TD1</code> and <code>REF</code>.</li>
<li>the <code>HL</code> segment repeats once more when the order contains an item, and the item itself is described by the segments <code>LIN</code>, <code>SN1</code>, and <code>PID</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="add-an-hl-loop-to-your-guide"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#add-an-hl-loop-to-your-guide"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Add an HL loop to your guide</a></h4>
<p>X12 does not enforce a specific hierarchy in your transaction set. You can add <code>HL</code> loops to your Stedi guide to define the hierarchical relationships you need for your use case.</p>
<p>You must add <code>HL</code> loops to your guides one level at a time. For example, you would create three nested <code>HL</code> segments to capture the following hierarchy.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>Order</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ├── Package</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      ├── Item</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>To add an <code>HL</code> loop for this scenario:</p>
<ol>
<li>Click the <strong>DETAIL</strong> heading in the left sidebar.</li>
<li>Click the box next to the HL Loop to change its status from <strong>Not Used</strong>.</li>
<li>Choose a code to describe the type of entry for this level of the hierarchy. In this example, you would choose <code>O</code> for order.</li>
<li>Click <strong>Save</strong> to add the HL segment under <strong>DETAIL</strong>.</li>
<li>Click the HL Loop, scroll to the list of HL segments.</li>
<li>Click the box next to <strong>HL Loop</strong> to add it and select a code. In this example, you&#x27;d select <code>P</code> for package.</li>
<li>Repeat this process for the final hierarchy level describing the item.</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="hl-loop-variations"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#hl-loop-variations"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>HL Loop Variations</a></h4>
<p>Sometimes, an implementation guide allows for variations of a hierarchy. For example, if a ship notice only has one package, you can leave out the package information.</p>
<p>You can convey this information to your trading partners by creating <a href="#variants">variants</a> within a single Stedi guide or by creating a separate Stedi guide for each variant.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="variants"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#variants"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Variants</a></h3>
<p>Loops and segments allow you to create variants. A variant is a specific version of a loop or a segment that is used in a particular context.</p>
<p>To create a variant, go to the segment and click <strong>+ Create variant</strong> under the <strong>Variant group</strong> section.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="variant-sequence"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#variant-sequence"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Variant sequence</a></h4>
<p>Some trading partners require that you send certain iterations of loops or segments before others. To address these requirements, specify the <strong>Variant sequence</strong>, or position number, for each variant. This approach ensures that the variants appear in a specific order when you use this guide to write EDI.</p>
<p>Variants with lower numbers are written before higher numbers, and variants without a defined sequence are written last.</p>
<p>You can only set the variant sequence for loops or segments with a variant defined. To set the variant sequence, click the loop or segment you want to edit and open the <strong>Advanced</strong> menu.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="discriminants"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#discriminants"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Discriminants</a></h4>
<p>Variants must be uniquely identifiable from each other. To do this, you must add a discriminant that differentiates each variant. The discriminant tells Stedi when one variant should be used over the other for validating, generating, or parsing EDI documents.</p>
<p>For example, you could specify that partners include two <code>N1 Name</code> loops in each <code>850</code> Purchase Order: one for the ship to contact and another for the bill to party. In this case you&#x27;d add the Entity Identifier Code as the discriminant for <code>N1 Name</code> loops. For the <code>bill to</code> variant, you&#x27;d use the <code>BT</code> qualifier, and for the ship to variant, you&#x27;d use the <code>ST</code> qualifier.</p>
<p>The type of discriminant depends on whether the loop is hierarchical:</p>
<ul>
<li>For hierarchical loops (HL loops), set a unique HL Level Code (<code>HL-03</code>) on each variant.</li>
<li>For non-hierarchical loops and segments, set a unique allowed value on each variant.</li>
</ul>
<p>You do not need to place the discriminant on the first element of the first segment. You can place it in any required element of the first segment. The only requirement is that the discriminant must be unique amongst all variants.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="elements"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#elements"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Elements</a></h2>
<p>By default, the guide builder only includes the <a href="https://www.stedi.com/docs/edi-platform/edi-essentials/x12/elements/what-is-an-element" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">elements</a> for each segment that are required in the base transaction set. You can add additional elements to your custom guide.</p>
<p>To add or remove elements from a segment:</p>
<ol>
<li>Click the segment&#x27;s name and scroll to find the list of possible elements.</li>
<li>Click the box next to each element to change whether it is included in the segment.</li>
</ol>
<span class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg flex gap-3 border border-emerald-100 bg-emerald-50 dark:border-emerald-950 dark:bg-emerald-500/10" data-callout-type="tip"><span class="flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-6 flex items-center justify-center text-emerald-700 dark:text-emerald-300" data-component-part="callout-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon "><path d="M11 18H7.94101C7.64391 16.7274 6.30412 15.6857 5.75395 14.9992C4.65645 13.6297 4 11.8915 4 10C4 5.58172 7.58172 2 12 2C16.4183 2 20 5.58172 20 10C20 11.8925 19.3428 13.6315 18.2443 15.0014C17.6944 15.687 16.3558 16.7276 16.059 18H13V13H11V18ZM16 20V21C16 22.1046 15.1046 23 14 23H10C8.89543 23 8 22.1046 8 21V20H16Z"></path></svg></span><span class="prose min-w-0 w-full text-emerald-900 dark:text-emerald-200" data-component-part="callout-content"><p>Some PDF guides have elements marked as conditional (<code>X</code>). These have special
rules associated with them. At this step, you should mark them as optional.</p></span></span>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="conditional-elements"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#conditional-elements"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Conditional elements</a></h3>
<p>Some elements come with conditions that tell you when they should be included. For example, if you specify a date in the <a href="https://www.stedi.com/edi/x12/segment/G62" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">date/time-segment</a>, you must also specify a date qualifier. Similarly, if you specify a time, you must also specify a time qualifier. You can specify either a date or a time, but you must include at least one.</p>
<p>Every condition begins with a letter that specifies the type of condition, followed by one or more element numbers to which the condition applies. For example, <code>R0103</code> means that you must specify at least one of the elements <code>01</code> or <code>03</code>.</p>
<p>It’s possible to specify more than two elements, so <code>R010304</code> would mean that you must specify at least one of the elements <code>01</code>, <code>03</code>, or <code>04</code>.</p>
<div class="relative overflow-auto prose-no-margin my-6"><table><thead><tr><th><strong>Letter</strong></th><th><strong>Name</strong></th><th><strong>Condition</strong></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>C</code></td><td>Condition</td><td>If the first element is present, then all the other elements must be present.</td></tr><tr><td><code>E</code></td><td>Exclusive</td><td>Only one of the elements may be present.</td></tr><tr><td><code>L</code></td><td>List conditional</td><td>If the first element is present, then at least one of the other elements must be present.</td></tr><tr><td><code>P</code></td><td>Paired</td><td>If one of the elements is present, then all elements must be present.</td></tr><tr><td><code>R</code></td><td>Required</td><td>At least one of the elements must be present.</td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="add-conditions"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#add-conditions"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Add Conditions</a></h4>
<p>You must specify conditions for elements on the segment level. To add conditions:</p>
<ol>
<li>Click the segment name in the left sidebar.</li>
<li>Scroll to the <strong>Conditions</strong> section in the center column and click <strong>+ Add condition</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<span class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg flex gap-3 border border-emerald-100 bg-emerald-50 dark:border-emerald-950 dark:bg-emerald-500/10" data-callout-type="tip"><span class="flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-6 flex items-center justify-center text-emerald-700 dark:text-emerald-300" data-component-part="callout-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon "><path d="M11 18H7.94101C7.64391 16.7274 6.30412 15.6857 5.75395 14.9992C4.65645 13.6297 4 11.8915 4 10C4 5.58172 7.58172 2 12 2C16.4183 2 20 5.58172 20 10C20 11.8925 19.3428 13.6315 18.2443 15.0014C17.6944 15.687 16.3558 16.7276 16.059 18H13V13H11V18ZM16 20V21C16 22.1046 15.1046 23 14 23H10C8.89543 23 8 22.1046 8 21V20H16Z"></path></svg></span><span class="prose min-w-0 w-full text-emerald-900 dark:text-emerald-200" data-component-part="callout-content"><p>Learn more about <a href="/docs/edi-platform/edi-essentials/x12/elements/relational-conditions-in-x12-edi">X12 EDI relational
conditions</a>
in our EDI Reference documentation.</p></span></span>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="data-type-and-length"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#data-type-and-length"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Data type and length</a></h3>
<p>Every element has a specific data type and length. Your guide automatically copies the data type and length settings from the base specification for the transaction set. Implementation guides typically use the same data type and length as the base specification, so we recommend leaving the default settings as is, unless you have a specific reason for updating them.</p>
<p>To edit the element&#x27;s data type, click the element name in the sidebar and open the <strong>Advanced</strong> menu in the center column.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="maximum-length-of-numeric-elements"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#maximum-length-of-numeric-elements"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Maximum length of numeric elements</a></h4>
<p>Numeric elements in Stedi Guides have a maximum length of 15. This differs from the X12 specification, which does not enforce a maximum length for numeric data element types. The reason for this discrepancy is that most common programming languages and libraries deserialize JSON numbers to double precision floating point numbers, which have a maximum of 15 digits of precision. This maximum length ensures that numbers do not have their value changed in the process.</p>
<p>By default, Guides has reduced the length of certain X12 data elements to improve usability. For example, X12 element <code>[212 Unit Price](https://www.stedi.com/edi/x12/element/212)</code> has a maximum length of 17. In Guides, this is reduced to 15 by default, since very few use cases legitimately require 17 digits of pricing precision.</p>
<p>If you need additional digits of precision, you can always change a numeric field to a string, which allows you to choose an arbitrary length.</p>
<p>When working with numbers where precision is important, we recommend deserializing to decimal types with the appropriate precision for your business case.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="allowed-values"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#allowed-values"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Allowed values</a></h3>
<p>Many elements have a value based on a standardized list of codes. For example, the date/time segment has the date qualifier segment, which indicates the type of date to include. The base specifiation lists well over a hundred possible codes. The implementation guide should list which ones are valid for you.</p>
<p>To update the list of accepted codes for an element:</p>
<ol>
<li>Click the element&#x27;s name in the left sidebar.</li>
<li>Scroll to the <strong>Allowed values</strong> section in the center column and click <strong>+ Add code value</strong>.</li>
<li>Add one or more codes that are appropriate for your use cases.</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="delimiters"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#delimiters"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Delimiters</a></h2>
<p>Delimiters separate the segments and elements in an EDI file.</p>
<p>When you create a guide, you can set delimiters in the <em>Overview</em> pane in the top left. Stedi uses the guide&#x27;s delimiters when <a href="/docs/edi-platform/operate/generate-edi">writing EDI</a>.
As a default, Stedi recommends the following choices:</p>
<ul>
<li>Element: <code>*</code></li>
<li>Segment: <code>~</code></li>
<li>Repetition: <code>^</code></li>
<li>Component Element: <code>&gt;</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Other common choices for the component element include <code>:</code>, <code>&lt;</code>, and <code>\</code>.</p>
<p>Choosing delimiters for reading and writing EDI depends on your and your trading partner&#x27;s data requirements. Clearly communicate the character restrictions with the business groups that are sending the data. You should also agree on substitution characters when a delimiter appears in the data. For example, if your delimiter is <code>*</code> and you know incoming data contains mathematical expressions, you could agree to use <code>x</code> instead of <code>*</code> for relevant expressions (<code>4x2</code> instead of <code>4*2</code>).</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="writing-edi"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#writing-edi"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Writing EDI</a></h3>
<p>Stedi will parse your data incorrectly if the delimiter you choose appears elsewhere in your data. For example, if your input uses mathematical symbols, then we recommend choosing <code>:</code> or <code>\</code> instead of <code>&gt;</code> and <code>&lt;</code> as delimiters. Likewise, you may want to avoid <code>:</code> if your text data includes time values in <code>HH:MM:SS</code> format. We recommend considering the following guidance from the X12 documentation.</p>
<p>The following characters usually occur in data. They should not be used as delimiters:</p>
<ul>
<li>Upper (<code>A-Z</code>) and lowercase (<code>a-z</code>) letters</li>
<li>Digits (<code>0-9</code>)</li>
<li>Blank space (<code> </code>)</li>
<li>Minus sign (<code>-</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>The following characters often appear in data. Use as delimiter characters with caution.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>&quot; ! &amp; &#x27; ( ) * + , - . / : ; ? =</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The following characters sometimes appear in data. Use as delimiter characters with caution.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>% @ [ ] \_ { } \ | &lt; &gt; ~ ^ `</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="reading-edi"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#reading-edi"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Reading EDI</a></h3>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="delimiters-1"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#delimiters-1"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Delimiters</a></h4>
<p>We recommend allowing your trading partners to use any type of delimiter when sending data. They may have different data requirements and have likely already worked to ensure there are no conflicts with EDI delimiters.</p>
<p>Stedi automatically infers the delimiters from incoming EDI files.</p>
<h4 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="x12-guidance-for-delimiters"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#x12-guidance-for-delimiters"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>X12 guidance for delimiters</a></h4>
<p>X12 provides the following guidance about delimiters.</p>
<p>The following characters usually occur in data. They should not be used as delimiters:</p>
<ul>
<li>Upper (<code>A-Z</code>) and lowercase (<code>a-z</code>) letters</li>
<li>Digits (<code>0-9</code>)</li>
<li>Blank space (<code> </code>)</li>
<li>Minus sign (<code>-</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>The following characters often appear in data. Use as delimiter characters with caution.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>&quot; ! &amp; &#x27; ( ) \* + , - . / : ; ? =</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>The following characters sometimes appear in data. Use as delimiter characters with caution.</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="code-block not-prose group relative my-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border text-sm outline-none !bg-black h-auto [--shiki-light:#D4D4D4] [--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4] shiki shiki-themes stedi-custom stedi-custom" style="--shiki-light:#D4D4D4;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4;--shiki-light-bg:#0A0A0A;--shiki-dark-bg:#0A0A0A" tabindex="0"><button aria-label="Copy Text" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 bg-transparent hover:bg-transparent hover:text-gray-100 cursor-pointer absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] text-quaternary" type="button"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 20.9998 2.44772 20.9998 3V17C20.9998 17.5523 20.5521 18 19.9998 18H16.9998V20.9991C16.9998 21.5519 16.5499 22 15.993 22H4.00666C3.45059 22 3 21.5554 3 20.9991L3.0026 7.00087C3.0027 6.44811 3.45264 6 4.00942 6H6.9998ZM5.00242 8L5.00019 20H14.9998V8H5.00242ZM8.9998 6H16.9998V16H18.9998V4H8.9998V6Z"></path></svg></button><div class="text-[13px] py-3.5 overflow-auto [&amp;_.line]:px-4 fd-scroll-container h-full"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>% @ [ ] \_ { } \ | &lt; &gt; ~ ^ `</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="attachments"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#attachments"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Attachments</a></h2>
<p>You can attach files to any Stedi guide and choose whether the attachments are public or private (only available to members of your Stedi account).</p>
<p>For example, you may want to add private attachments that help your team debug issues in your EDI pipeline, such as the original PDF specifications or a changelog. For a public guide, you may want to attach an appendix with a supplementary code list or a diagram that helps your partners understand the messaging flow.</p>
<p>To add attachments to a guide in your account, navigate to its <strong>Overview</strong> page, scroll to the <strong>Attachments</strong> section, and click <strong>Attach file</strong>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="sample-edi-files-for-public-guides"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#sample-edi-files-for-public-guides"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Sample EDI files for public guides</a></h2>
<p>You can include multiple EDI sample files in Stedi guides to help new trading partners understand valid usage patterns faster and reduce onboarding time. The guide builder automatically validates each sample against the guide&#x27;s specifications, so you can fix any errors before you provide them to trading partners.</p>
<p>You can also add a description to each sample that gives trading partners even more context about the intended use cases. The description appears at the top of the guide&#x27;s EDI Inspector.</p>
<p>To add samples:</p>
<ol>
<li>Click <strong>Overview</strong> in the left sidebar and scroll to the <strong>EDI Samples</strong> section in the center column. Click on <strong>+ Add Sample</strong>.</li>
<li>In the <strong>EDI Sample</strong> tab, add a <strong>Name</strong> and paste a sample file or customize an autogenerated sample based on the guide&#x27;s specifications.</li>
<li>You may add an an optional <strong>Description</strong> in the <strong>Description</strong> tab.</li>
<li>Click <strong>Create sample</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<p>EDI samples attached to the guide are used:</p>
<ol>
<li>In the <a href="/docs/edi-platform/operate/generate-test-files">Generate EDI test file</a> flow.</li>
<li>On your <a href="/docs/edi-platform/guides/public-guides">public guide&#x27;s</a> interactive web page and are included when partners download the guide as a PDF.</li>
</ol></div><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4 empty:hidden"></div><div class="grid w-full grid-cols-2 gap-4 py-8 md:py-10 border-t border-secondary" This differs from the X12 specification, which does not enforce a maximum length for numeric data element types. The reason for this discrepancy is that most common programming languages and libraries deserialize JSON numbers to double precision floating point numbers, which have a maximum of 15 digits of precision. This maximum length ensures that numbers do not have their value changed in the process.\"}]\n7a:[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"By default, Guides has reduced the length of certain X12 data elements to improve usability.
